I really like this store. Being new to gardening and having more questions than money didn't deter Taylor or Tony from patiently answering all of my questions. I appreciate that.

<Pictures>None< /Pictures>< text>
I alternate between giving Bombay four or five stars. When they are good, they are really good! In fact they are easily the best Indian restaurant in San Diego, perhaps all of Southern California! And yes I've tried all the others including several others in Hillcrest and a bunch of them off of Miramar Road. Bombay is awesome, the food is phenomenal and the setting and Ambience are incredible with water features and lighting and beautiful authentic decor. Only minus is that sometimes the staff could be a bit more attentive, IA your glass can sit empty for a couple of minutes before anyone notices you want a refill but other than sleep labs in service this is an awesome amazing restaurant that features a daily lunch buffet at a very reasonable price! Oh, and this is owned by a local family, not a huge restaurant chain so go and support local restaurateurs!</text>

< Review>
First impression, "wow." The interior of the resturant is beautiful with ceiling waterfall and many decorative pieces, such as statues and gas lit lamps, with an exotic dancer.
First impression of the waitor, "she's really nice and humble." Gave good recommendations and was so sweet.
BUT THE SERVICE, THO
Unlike the lamps, it was not lit. We waited a little over an hour for our food. As we sat there hungry we saw people getting served left and right. If I were alone I would have got up and left to hit the nearest Denny's, but since it was girls' night out I stayed. The problem was, they forgot about us and we didn't get a free appetizer, dessert, nor did we get a discount. The waitor apologize and explained honestly that the servers never came out, forgetting about us. The food was warm, and we were disappointed.
As we proceed to check out we waited an extra 20 minutes just to pay for our bill.
Never coming back. Not bom(bay) at all.< /Review>

< Review>
I ate at Bombay last night and can't believe they are trying to defend themselves with this nonsense (comment from 9/19/10).  Instead of posting comments claiming the bad reviews are lies, I suggest you go eat some of your food.  Chicken tikka masala that is dry!  I don't know how you can even do that!  Hard dry chunks of chicken in a flavorless tomato sauce.  The seeka kabobs, allo gobi and nan were OK but the prices are way too high for so/so to bad food.  On the flip side the decor in the new restaurant is amazing.  Now turn off your computer and go work on your food because I'll be trying the place across the street before I step food in Bombay again.  And I also agree with the earlier comment, Black Mtn Rd Indian restaurants are all much better (I'll take food over decor any day.)<//Review>

<date>1541732271687< /date>< rating>
3</rating>
< review>
Best vape shop in Atwater which isn't saying much. They have a decent selection and most things are in stock most of the time but they are popular so it makes sense that they'd run out of something but usually they'll have it in the next day or so. As for the prices, well, it's typical of vape shops to be way over priced compared to online and this one is no different. The main dude that works most of the time is cool but his little helper is an angry little man with an attitude who has absolutely zero knowledge about any of the products they sell. If you don't believe me just go in there and ask him a question about anything that you already know the answer to and you will either ask the main guy who usually knows or he'll give you some bogus response half the time. For example if you're looking for a coil for your atomizer (it better be smok or compatible with baby beast or prince cuz that's all they have) he seems to think they are all universally compatible. If you don't need whatever you're trying to buy immediately it's best to just shop online and save your money.<//review>

< Name>

1456814731155<//Date>
< rate>
5< /rate>
< text>
God is doing great things at Liberty. The church is so friendly!
Pastor Thomson brings a well balanced biblical message Sunday morning, evening and Wednesday night. The gospel is central in the messages. Typically Sunday mornings have a series that's very practical for the believer. Pastor is a very good bible teacher. He uses relevant illustrations, quotes, visuals and humor to keep you engaged and to help you understand the Word.
Worship is a balance of songs and hymns that are engaging and fresh. The choir is growing. Singing specials are very well done and allow many more members than just the choir to sing and bless the church.
The connection groups for college students on Sunday morning (Sunday school) have that small group, everyone can share, intimate feeling, yet are still structured.
One-on-one discipleship is also a great way to sit down and learn from another Christian about the Bible and to build relationships. It is very much encouraged for you to read the Word on your own, rather than just receive what a man says. There is a careful balance of seeking knowledge and having a heart relationship with God and here you'll find you can grow in both.
There are many opportunities to serve and get involved in a ministry that reaches people with the gospel.
The graphic design and visuals are all very high end and professional.
There is also a large growing Spanish ministry.
I am a student at UCI and there is a good singles/college group at the church campus, though a presence on college campus would be helpful.< /text>

<rating>5< /rating>< review>
I use this pool for adult lap swimming. Busy during the summer while students are out on vacation but relatively relaxed during the school year during adult lap swim hours (except for Fridays, which are busy).

Purchase a lap pass for ~$80 and you get 30 visits at a discounted price vs paying each time. The pool is (relatively) clean and the showers are warm enough.</review>

<Name>Alex Pacura<//Name><time>1550425785785<//time><rate>5</rate>< review>
I moved to this area 4 months ago and people have mentioned this place to me but I never went. In an attempt to make a home made kale salad I needed to find bunches of kale that were not pre cut and bagged like trader Joe's and aldi have.
Well, I found everything I needed at vons. They have the best selection of organic and conventional vegetables in the area. This was surprising because you imagine trader joe's as a place to get healthy food but it's all processed and bagged up in plastic.
Before vons I was getting really disappointed with the quality of food in socal. I can now say vons is restoring my hope in this place.
After buying my kale bunches I went home, washed and cut the kale leaves myself. Then I made a delicious dressing. Also I found real balsamic vinegar at vons. Trader Joe's also has balsamic vinegar but it all has caramel food coloring in it.
Well because of vons I was able to get all the ingredients for my kale salad and then enjoy it for dinner.
Lastly something I've been searching for at all the stores, wholefoods, sprouts stores in the area for the last 4 months I found at vons. This is beef liver. If you need a source of beef liver vons is it.
Thanks,
Alex</review>
